      1 +"""Core Connect 4 game state backed by bitboards."""
      2 +
      3 +from __future__ import annotations
      4 +
      5 +from dataclasses import dataclass
      6 +from typing import Iterable
      7 +
      8 +import numpy as np
      9 +
     10 +from .constants import (
     11 +    BITS_PER_COLUMN,
     12 +    DEFAULT_MOVE_ORDER,
     13 +    HEIGHT,
     14 +    MAX_MOVES,
     15 +    PLAYER1,
     16 +    PLAYER2,
     17 +    WIDTH,
     18 +)
     19 +
     20 +
     21 +def bottom_mask(column: int) -> int:
     22 +    return 1 << (column * BITS_PER_COLUMN)
     23 +
     24 +
     25 +def column_mask(column: int) -> int:
     26 +    return ((1 << HEIGHT) - 1) << (column * BITS_PER_COLUMN)
     27 +
     28 +
     29 +def top_mask(column: int) -> int:
     30 +    return 1 << (HEIGHT - 1 + column * BITS_PER_COLUMN)
     31 +
     32 +
     33 +BOTTOM_MASK_ALL = sum(bottom_mask(column) for column in range(WIDTH))
     34 +BOARD_MASK = sum(column_mask(column) for column in range(WIDTH))
     35 +
     36 +
     37 +def has_alignment(bitboard: int) -> bool:
     38 +    for shift in (1, BITS_PER_COLUMN, BITS_PER_COLUMN - 1, BITS_PER_COLUMN + 1)
         :
     39 +        m = bitboard & (bitboard >> shift)
     40 +        if m & (m >> (2 * shift)):
     41 +            return True
     42 +    return False
     43 +
     44 +
     45 +@dataclass(frozen=True, slots=True)
     46 +class Connect4State:
     47 +    """Immutable Connect 4 position.
     48 +
     49 +    `current_position` always stores stones for the side to move.
     50 +    `mask` stores occupied cells for both players.
     51 +    """
     52 +
     53 +    current_position: int = 0
     54 +    mask: int = 0
     55 +    move_count: int = 0
     56 +    history: tuple[int, ...] = ()
     57 +
     58 +    @property
     59 +    def to_play(self) -> int:
     60 +        return PLAYER1 if self.move_count % 2 == 0 else PLAYER2
     61 +
     62 +    @property
     63 +    def opponent_position(self) -> int:
     64 +        return self.mask ^ self.current_position
     65 +
     66 +    def can_play(self, column: int) -> bool:
     67 +        return 0 <= column < WIDTH and (self.mask & top_mask(column)) == 0
     68 +
     69 +    def legal_moves(self) -> list[int]:
     70 +        return [column for column in DEFAULT_MOVE_ORDER if self.can_play(column
         )]
     71 +
     72 +    def move_bit(self, column: int) -> int:
     73 +        return (self.mask + bottom_mask(column)) & column_mask(column)
     74 +
     75 +    def is_winning_move(self, column: int) -> bool:
     76 +        if not self.can_play(column):
     77 +            return False
     78 +        return has_alignment(self.current_position | self.move_bit(column))
     79 +
     80 +    def play(self, column: int) -> "Connect4State":
     81 +        if not self.can_play(column):
     82 +            raise ValueError(f"illegal move: column {column}")
     83 +        move = self.move_bit(column)
     84 +        return Connect4State(
     85 +            current_position=self.current_position ^ self.mask,
     86 +            mask=self.mask | move,
     87 +            move_count=self.move_count + 1,
     88 +            history=self.history + (column,),
     89 +        )
     90 +
     91 +    def is_draw(self) -> bool:
     92 +        return self.move_count >= MAX_MOVES and not self.last_move_won()
     93 +
     94 +    def last_move_won(self) -> bool:
     95 +        if self.move_count == 0:
     96 +            return False
     97 +        return has_alignment(self.opponent_position)
     98 +
     99 +    def is_terminal(self) -> bool:
    100 +        return self.last_move_won() or self.move_count >= MAX_MOVES
    101 +
    102 +    def outcome_for_player_to_move(self) -> int:
    103 +        if self.last_move_won():
    104 +            return -1
    105 +        if self.move_count >= MAX_MOVES:
    106 +            return 0
    107 +        raise ValueError("position is not terminal")
    108 +
    109 +    def winner(self) -> int | None:
    110 +        if not self.last_move_won():
    111 +            return None
    112 +        return -self.to_play
    113 +
    114 +    def board_array(self) -> np.ndarray:
    115 +        board = np.zeros((HEIGHT, WIDTH), dtype=np.int8)
    116 +        player_to_move = self.current_position
    117 +        opponent = self.opponent_position
    118 +        for column in range(WIDTH):
    119 +            base = column * BITS_PER_COLUMN
    120 +            for row in range(HEIGHT):
    121 +                bit = 1 << (base + row)
    122 +                if player_to_move & bit:
    123 +                    board[row, column] = self.to_play
    124 +                elif opponent & bit:
    125 +                    board[row, column] = -self.to_play
    126 +        return board
    127 +
    128 +    def encoded(self) -> np.ndarray:
    129 +        board = self.board_array()
    130 +        current = (board == self.to_play).astype(np.float32)
    131 +        opponent = (board == -self.to_play).astype(np.float32)
    132 +        turn = np.full((HEIGHT, WIDTH), 1.0 if self.to_play == PLAYER1 else 0.0
         , dtype=np.float32)
    133 +        return np.stack([current, opponent, turn], axis=0)
    134 +
    135 +    def mirror(self) -> "Connect4State":
    136 +        mirrored = []
    137 +        for move in self.history:
    138 +            mirrored.append(WIDTH - 1 - move)
    139 +        return Connect4State.from_moves(mirrored)
    140 +
    141 +    def pretty(self, use_color: bool = True) -> str:
    142 +        board = self.board_array()
    143 +        red = "\033[31m"
    144 +        yellow = "\033[33m"
    145 +        reset = "\033[0m"
    146 +        lines = ["  1   2   3   4   5   6   7"]
    147 +        lines.append("+---+---+---+---+---+---+---+")
    148 +        for row in range(HEIGHT - 1, -1, -1):
    149 +            cells = []
    150 +            for column in range(WIDTH):
    151 +                value = board[row, column]
    152 +                if value == PLAYER1:
    153 +                    token = "R"
    154 +                    if use_color:
    155 +                        token = f"{red}O{reset}"
    156 +                elif value == PLAYER2:
    157 +                    token = "Y"
    158 +                    if use_color:
    159 +                        token = f"{yellow}O{reset}"
    160 +                else:
    161 +                    token = "."
    162 +                cells.append(f" {token} ")
    163 +            lines.append("|" + "|".join(cells) + "|")
    164 +            lines.append("+---+---+---+---+---+---+---+")
    165 +        return "\n".join(lines)
    166 +
    167 +    @classmethod
    168 +    def from_moves(cls, moves: Iterable[int]) -> "Connect4State":
    169 +        state = cls()
    170 +        for move in moves:
    171 +            state = state.play(int(move))
    172 +        return state

  └ connect4_az/solver.py (+223 -0)
      1 +"""Exact solver and training labels for Connect 4."""
      2 +
      3 +from __future__ import annotations
      4 +
      5 +from dataclasses import dataclass
      6 +from functools import lru_cache
      7 +from typing import Iterable
      8 +
      9 +from .constants import BITS_PER_COLUMN, DEFAULT_MOVE_ORDER, HEIGHT, MAX_MOVES,
         WIDTH
     10 +from .game import BOARD_MASK, BOTTOM_MASK_ALL, Connect4State, has_alignment
     11 +
     12 +
     13 +def _possible_mask(mask: int) -> int:
     14 +    return (mask + BOTTOM_MASK_ALL) & BOARD_MASK
     15 +
     16 +
     17 +def _winning_positions(position: int, mask: int) -> int:
     18 +    result = 0
     19 +
     20 +    # Vertical
     21 +    result |= (position << 1) & (position << 2) & (position << 3)
     22 +
     23 +    # Horizontal
     24 +    shift = BITS_PER_COLUMN
     25 +    p = (position << shift) & (position << (2 * shift))
     26 +    result |= p & (position << (3 * shift))
     27 +    result |= p & (position >> shift)
     28 +    p = (position >> shift) & (position >> (2 * shift))
     29 +    result |= p & (position << shift)
     30 +    result |= p & (position >> (3 * shift))
     31 +
     32 +    # Diagonal /
     33 +    shift = BITS_PER_COLUMN - 1
     34 +    p = (position << shift) & (position << (2 * shift))
     35 +    result |= p & (position << (3 * shift))
     36 +    result |= p & (position >> shift)
     37 +    p = (position >> shift) & (position >> (2 * shift))
     38 +    result |= p & (position << shift)
     39 +    result |= p & (position >> (3 * shift))
     40 +
     41 +    # Diagonal \
     42 +    shift = BITS_PER_COLUMN + 1
     43 +    p = (position << shift) & (position << (2 * shift))
     44 +    result |= p & (position << (3 * shift))
     45 +    result |= p & (position >> shift)
     46 +    p = (position >> shift) & (position >> (2 * shift))
     47 +    result |= p & (position << shift)
     48 +    result |= p & (position >> (3 * shift))
     49 +
     50 +    return result & (BOARD_MASK ^ mask)
     51 +
     52 +
     53 +def _move_score(move: int) -> int:
     54 +    if move == 3:
     55 +        return 6
     56 +    return 5 - abs(3 - move)
     57 +
     58 +
     59 +@dataclass(slots=True)
     60 +class ExactSolver:
     61 +    """Negamax alpha-beta solver with memoization.
     62 +
     63 +    Values use the standard Connect 4 exact score convention:
     64 +    positive means the side to move has a forced win,
     65 +    zero means draw,
     66 +    negative means forced loss.
     67 +    Magnitude is distance-to-terminal aware, which helps move ranking.
     68 +    """
     69 +
     70 +    cache_size: int = 4_000_000
     71 +
     72 +    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
     73 +        self._table: dict[tuple[int, int], int] = {}
     74 +
     75 +    def clear(self) -> None:
     76 +        self._table.clear()
     77 +
     78 +    def possible_non_losing_moves(self, state: Connect4State) -> list[int]:
     79 +        if state.is_terminal():
     80 +            return []
     81 +        possible = _possible_mask(state.mask)
     82 +        opponent_win = _winning_positions(state.opponent_position, state.mask)
     83 +        forced = possible & opponent_win
     84 +        if forced:
     85 +            if forced & (forced - 1):
     86 +                return []
     87 +            possible = forced
     88 +        possible &= ~(opponent_win >> 1)
     89 +        moves = []
     90 +        for move in DEFAULT_MOVE_ORDER:
     91 +            move_bit = state.move_bit(move) if state.can_play(move) else 0
     92 +            if move_bit and (possible & move_bit):
     93 +                moves.append(move)
     94 +        return moves
     95 +
     96 +    def solve(self, state: Connect4State) -> int:
     97 +        return self._negamax(state.current_position, state.mask)
     98 +
     99 +    def move_scores(self, state: Connect4State) -> dict[int, int]:
    100 +        if state.is_terminal():
    101 +            return {}
    102 +        scores: dict[int, int] = {}
    103 +        legal_moves = state.legal_moves()
    104 +        for move in legal_moves:
    105 +            child = state.play(move)
    106 +            if child.last_move_won():
    107 +                scores[move] = (MAX_MOVES + 1 - state.move_count) // 2
    108 +            else:
    109 +                scores[move] = -self.solve(child)
    110 +        return scores
    111 +
    112 +    def best_moves(self, state: Connect4State) -> list[int]:
    113 +        scores = self.move_scores(state)
    114 +        if not scores:
    115 +            return []
    116 +        best = max(scores.values())
    117 +        return sorted([move for move, score in scores.items() if score == best]
         )
    118 +
    119 +    def policy_target(self, state: Connect4State, temperature: float = 1.0) ->
         list[float]:
    120 +        scores = self.move_scores(state)
    121 +        policy = [0.0] * WIDTH
    122 +        if not scores:
    123 +            return policy
    124 +        best = max(scores.values())
    125 +        if temperature <= 0:
    126 +            best_moves = [move for move, score in scores.items() if score == be
         st]
    127 +            mass = 1.0 / len(best_moves)
    128 +            for move in best_moves:
    129 +                policy[move] = mass
    130 +            return policy
    131 +        weights = []
    132 +        for move in range(WIDTH):
    133 +            if move not in scores:
    134 +                weights.append(0.0)
    135 +                continue
    136 +            margin = scores[move] - best
    137 +            weights.append(float(pow(2.718281828, margin / max(temperature, 1e-
         6))))
    138 +        total = sum(weights)
    139 +        if total <= 0:
    140 +            return self.policy_target(state, temperature=0.0)
    141 +        for move in range(WIDTH):
    142 +            policy[move] = weights[move] / total
    143 +        return policy
    144 +
    145 +    def _negamax(self, current_position: int, mask: int, alpha: int | None = No
         ne, beta: int | None = None) -> int:
    146 +        move_count = mask.bit_count()
    147 +        if move_count >= MAX_MOVES:
    148 +            return 0
    149 +
    150 +        possible = _possible_mask(mask)
    151 +        winning_moves = _winning_positions(current_position, mask) & possible
    152 +        if winning_moves:
    153 +            return (MAX_MOVES + 1 - move_count) // 2
    154 +
    155 +        opponent_position = mask ^ current_position
    156 +        opponent_winning = _winning_positions(opponent_position, mask)
    157 +        forced = possible & opponent_winning
    158 +        if forced:
    159 +            if forced & (forced - 1):
    160 +                return -((MAX_MOVES - move_count) // 2)
    161 +            possible = forced
    162 +
    163 +        possible &= ~(opponent_winning >> 1)
    164 +        if possible == 0:
    165 +            return -((MAX_MOVES - move_count) // 2)
    166 +
    167 +        max_score = (MAX_MOVES - 1 - move_count) // 2
    168 +        if alpha is None:
    169 +            alpha = -max_score
    170 +        if beta is None:
    171 +            beta = max_score
    172 +        beta = min(beta, max_score)
    173 +        if alpha >= beta:
    174 +            return beta
    175 +
    176 +        key = (current_position, mask)
    177 +        cached = self._table.get(key)
    178 +        if cached is not None:
    179 +            return cached
    180 +
    181 +        best = -max_score
    182 +        ordered_moves = []
    183 +        for move in DEFAULT_MOVE_ORDER:
    184 +            move_bit = (mask + (1 << (move * BITS_PER_COLUMN))) & (((1 << HEIGH
         T) - 1) << (move * BITS_PER_COLUMN))
    185 +            if move_bit and (possible & move_bit):
    186 +                ordered_moves.append((move, move_bit))
    187 +        ordered_moves.sort(key=lambda item: _move_score(item[0]), reverse=True)
    188 +
    189 +        for _, move_bit in ordered_moves:
    190 +            child_current = current_position ^ mask
    191 +            child_mask = mask | move_bit
    192 +            score = -self._negamax(child_current, child_mask, -beta, -alpha)
    193 +            if score >= beta:
    194 +                self._table[key] = score
    195 +                self._shrink_cache_if_needed()
    196 +                return score
    197 +            if score > best:
    198 +                best = score
    199 +            if score > alpha:
    200 +                alpha = score
    201 +
    202 +        self._table[key] = best
    203 +        self._shrink_cache_if_needed()
    204 +        return best
    205 +
    206 +    def _shrink_cache_if_needed(self) -> None:
    207 +        if len(self._table) <= self.cache_size:
    208 +            return
    209 +        for key in list(self._table.keys())[: self.cache_size // 4]:
    210 +            self._table.pop(key, None)
    211 +
    212 +
    213 +@lru_cache(maxsize=200_000)
    214 +def solved_value_from_moves(moves: tuple[int, ...]) -> int:
    215 +    solver = ExactSolver()
    216 +    return solver.solve(Connect4State.from_moves(moves))
    217 +
    218 +
    219 +def replay_outcome(moves: Iterable[int]) -> int:
    220 +    state = Connect4State.from_moves(moves)
    221 +    if state.is_terminal():
    222 +        return state.outcome_for_player_to_move()
    223 +    return ExactSolver().solve(state)

     17 +
     18 +_WORKER_SOLVER: ExactSolver | None = None
     19 +
     20 +
     21 +def _init_worker(cache_size: int) -> None:
     22 +    global _WORKER_SOLVER
     23 +    _WORKER_SOLVER = ExactSolver(cache_size=cache_size)
     24 +
     25 +
     26 +@dataclass(slots=True)
     27 +class GeneratedDataset:
     28 +    states: np.ndarray
     29 +    policy: np.ndarray
     30 +    value: np.ndarray
     31 +
     32 +    def save(self, path: str | Path) -> None:
     33 +        path = Path(path)
     34 +        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     35 +        np.savez_compressed(path, states=self.states, policy=self.policy, value
         =self.value)
     36 +
     37 +    @classmethod
     38 +    def load(cls, path: str | Path) -> "GeneratedDataset":
     39 +        data = np.load(Path(path))
     40 +        return cls(states=data["states"], policy=data["policy"], value=data["va
         lue"])
     41 +
     42 +
     43 +def _softmax(items: dict[int, int], temperature: float) -> list[float]:
     44 +    best = max(items.values())
     45 +    weights = [0.0] * WIDTH
     46 +    for move, score in items.items():
     47 +        weights[move] = math.exp((score - best) / max(temperature, 1e-6))
     48 +    total = sum(weights)
     49 +    return [weight / total if total > 0 else 0.0 for weight in weights]
     50 +
     51 +
     52 +def _sample_trajectory(seed: int) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
     53 +    assert _WORKER_SOLVER is not None
     54 +    rng = random.Random(seed)
     55 +    solver = _WORKER_SOLVER
     56 +    state = Connect4State()
     57 +
     58 +    # Diverse openings before switching to stronger play.
     59 +    opening_length = rng.randint(0, 8)
     60 +    for _ in range(opening_length):
     61 +        legal = state.legal_moves()
     62 +        if not legal:
     63 +            break
     64 +        weights = [4 - abs(3 - move) for move in legal]
     65 +        move = rng.choices(legal, weights=weights, k=1)[0]
     66 +        state = state.play(move)
     67 +        if state.is_terminal():
     68 +            break
     69 +
     70 +    states: list[np.ndarray] = []
     71 +    policies: list[np.ndarray] = []
     72 +    values: list[float] = []
     73 +
     74 +    while not state.is_terminal():
     75 +        scores = solver.move_scores(state)
     76 +        if not scores:
     77 +            break
     78 +        exact_value = solver.solve(state)
     79 +        states.append(state.encoded().astype(np.uint8))
     80 +        policies.append(np.asarray(solver.policy_target(state, temperature=0.55
         ), dtype=np.float32))
     81 +        values.append(float(max(-1.0, min(1.0, exact_value / 8.0))))
     82 +
     83 +        phase = rng.random()
     84 +        if phase < 0.55:
     85 +            probs = _softmax(scores, temperature=0.4 if state.move_count < 10 e
         lse 0.2)
     86 +            move = int(rng.choices(range(WIDTH), weights=probs, k=1)[0])
     87 +        elif phase < 0.85:
     88 +            best = max(scores.values())
     89 +            candidates = [move for move, score in scores.items() if score >= be
         st - 1]
     90 +            move = min(candidates, key=lambda c: abs(c - 3))
     91 +        else:
     92 +            legal = state.legal_moves()
     93 +            move = rng.choice(legal)
     94 +        if move not in scores:
     95 +            legal = state.legal_moves()
     96 +            move = rng.choice(legal)
     97 +        state = state.play(move)
     98 +
     99 +    augmented_states: list[np.ndarray] = []
    100 +    augmented_policies: list[np.ndarray] = []
    101 +    augmented_values: list[float] = []
    102 +    for encoded, policy, value in zip(states, policies, values, strict=True):
    103 +        augmented_states.append(encoded)
    104 +        augmented_policies.append(policy)
    105 +        augmented_values.append(value)
    106 +
    107 +        mirrored = np.flip(encoded, axis=2).copy()
    108 +        mirrored_policy = np.flip(policy, axis=0).copy()
    109 +        augmented_states.append(mirrored)
    110 +        augmented_policies.append(mirrored_policy)
    111 +        augmented_values.append(value)
    112 +
    113 +    if not augmented_states:
    114 +        return (
    115 +            np.empty((0, 3, 6, 7), dtype=np.uint8),
    116 +            np.empty((0, 7), dtype=np.float32),
    117 +            np.empty((0,), dtype=np.float32),
    118 +        )
    119 +
    120 +    return (
    121 +        np.stack(augmented_states).astype(np.uint8),
    122 +        np.stack(augmented_policies).astype(np.float32),
    123 +        np.asarray(augmented_values, dtype=np.float32),
    124 +    )
    125 +
    126 +
    127 +def generate_exact_dataset(
    128 +    samples: int,
    129 +    processes: int | None = None,
    130 +    worker_cache_size: int = 500_000,
    131 +    seed: int = 0,
    132 +) -> GeneratedDataset:
    133 +    processes = processes or max(1, mp.cpu_count() - 1)
    134 +    task_count = max(processes * 8, 64)
    135 +    seeds = [seed + offset for offset in range(task_count)]
    136 +    all_states: list[np.ndarray] = []
    137 +    all_policy: list[np.ndarray] = []
    138 +    all_value: list[np.ndarray] = []
    139 +    total = 0
    140 +
    141 +    with mp.get_context("spawn").Pool(
    142 +        processes=processes,
    143 +        initializer=_init_worker,
    144 +        initargs=(worker_cache_size,),
    145 +    ) as pool:
    146 +        next_seed = seed
    147 +        while total < samples:
    148 +            batch = [next_seed + index for index in range(task_count)]
    149 +            next_seed += task_count
    150 +            for states, policy, value in pool.imap_unordered(_sample_trajectory
         , batch, chunksize=2):
    151 +                if len(states) == 0:
    152 +                    continue
    153 +                remaining = samples - total
    154 +                take = min(remaining, len(states))
    155 +                all_states.append(states[:take])
    156 +                all_policy.append(policy[:take])
    157 +                all_value.append(value[:take])
    158 +                total += take
    159 +                if total >= samples:
    160 +                    break
    161 +
    162 +    return GeneratedDataset(
    163 +        states=np.concatenate(all_states, axis=0),
    164 +        policy=np.concatenate(all_policy, axis=0),
    165 +        value=np.concatenate(all_value, axis=0),
    166 +    )

      1 +"""PUCT Monte Carlo Tree Search."""
      2 +
      3 +from __future__ import annotations
      4 +
      5 +import math
      6 +from dataclasses import dataclass, field
      7 +
      8 +import numpy as np
      9 +import torch
     10 +
     11 +from .constants import WIDTH
     12 +from .game import Connect4State
     13 +from .model import PolicyValueNet
     14 +
     15 +
     16 +@dataclass(slots=True)
     17 +class MCTSConfig:
     18 +    simulations: int = 800
     19 +    c_puct: float = 1.5
     20 +    dirichlet_alpha: float = 0.3
     21 +    dirichlet_epsilon: float = 0.25
     22 +    temperature: float = 0.0
     23 +
     24 +
     25 +@dataclass
     26 +class Node:
     27 +    state: Connect4State
     28 +    prior: float = 1.0
     29 +    visit_count: int = 0
     30 +    value_sum: float = 0.0
     31 +    children: dict[int, "Node"] = field(default_factory=dict)
     32 +
     33 +    def value(self) -> float:
     34 +        if self.visit_count == 0:
     35 +            return 0.0
     36 +        return self.value_sum / self.visit_count
     37 +
     38 +    def expanded(self) -> bool:
     39 +        return bool(self.children)
     40 +
     41 +    def expand(self, priors: np.ndarray) -> None:
     42 +        for move in self.state.legal_moves():
     43 +            self.children[move] = Node(
     44 +                state=self.state.play(move),
     45 +                prior=float(priors[move]),
     46 +            )
     47 +
     48 +
     49 +def _masked_softmax(logits: torch.Tensor, legal_moves: list[int]) -> np.ndarray
         :
     50 +    mask = torch.full_like(logits, -1e9)
     51 +    for move in legal_moves:
     52 +        mask[..., move] = 0.0
     53 +    probs = torch.softmax(logits + mask, dim=-1)
     54 +    return probs.detach().cpu().numpy()
     55 +
     56 +
     57 +@torch.no_grad()
     58 +def evaluate_state(model: PolicyValueNet, state: Connect4State, device: torch.d
         evice) -> tuple[np.ndarray, float]:
     59 +    if state.is_terminal():
     60 +        priors = np.zeros(WIDTH, dtype=np.float32)
     61 +        return priors, float(state.outcome_for_player_to_move())
     62 +    tensor = torch.from_numpy(state.encoded()).unsqueeze(0).to(device=device, d
         type=torch.float32)
     63 +    logits, value = model(tensor)
     64 +    priors = _masked_softmax(logits[0], state.legal_moves())
     65 +    return priors.astype(np.float32), float(value.item())
     66 +
     67 +
     68 +def _add_dirichlet_noise(priors: np.ndarray, legal_moves: list[int], config: MC
         TSConfig) -> np.ndarray:
     69 +    if not legal_moves:
     70 +        return priors
     71 +    noise = np.random.dirichlet([config.dirichlet_alpha] * len(legal_moves))
     72 +    mixed = priors.copy()
     73 +    for idx, move in enumerate(legal_moves):
     74 +        mixed[move] = (1.0 - config.dirichlet_epsilon) * priors[move] + config.
         dirichlet_epsilon * noise[idx]
     75 +    return mixed
     76 +
     77 +
     78 +def _select_child(node: Node, config: MCTSConfig) -> tuple[int, Node]:
     79 +    best_score = -1e18
     80 +    best_move = -1
     81 +    best_child: Node | None = None
     82 +    sqrt_parent = math.sqrt(max(1, node.visit_count))
     83 +    for move, child in node.children.items():
     84 +        q_value = -child.value()
     85 +        u_value = config.c_puct * child.prior * sqrt_parent / (1 + child.visit_
         count)
     86 +        score = q_value + u_value
     87 +        if score > best_score:
     88 +            best_score = score
     89 +            best_move = move
     90 +            best_child = child
     91 +    assert best_child is not None
     92 +    return best_move, best_child
     93 +
     94 +
     95 +def run_mcts(
     96 +    model: PolicyValueNet,
     97 +    state: Connect4State,
     98 +    device: torch.device,
     99 +    config: MCTSConfig | None = None,
    100 +    add_noise: bool = False,
    101 +) -> tuple[list[float], int, Node]:
    102 +    config = config or MCTSConfig()
    103 +    root = Node(state=state)
    104 +    priors, value = evaluate_state(model, state, device)
    105 +    if not state.is_terminal():
    106 +        if add_noise:
    107 +            priors = _add_dirichlet_noise(priors, state.legal_moves(), config)
    108 +        root.expand(priors)
    109 +    root.visit_count = 1
    110 +    root.value_sum = value
    111 +
    112 +    for _ in range(config.simulations):
    113 +        node = root
    114 +        path = [node]
    115 +
    116 +        while node.expanded() and not node.state.is_terminal():
    117 +            _, node = _select_child(node, config)
    118 +            path.append(node)
    119 +
    120 +        if node.state.is_terminal():
    121 +            leaf_value = float(node.state.outcome_for_player_to_move())
    122 +        else:
    123 +            priors, leaf_value = evaluate_state(model, node.state, device)
    124 +            node.expand(priors)
    125 +
    126 +        value_to_propagate = leaf_value
    127 +        for visited in reversed(path):
    128 +            visited.visit_count += 1
    129 +            visited.value_sum += value_to_propagate
    130 +            value_to_propagate = -value_to_propagate
    131 +
    132 +    visits = [0.0] * WIDTH
    133 +    for move, child in root.children.items():
    134 +        visits[move] = float(child.visit_count)
    135 +
    136 +    move = select_move_from_visits(visits, state.legal_moves(), config.temperat
         ure)
    137 +    return visits, move, root
    138 +
    139 +
    140 +def select_move_from_visits(visits: list[float], legal_moves: list[int], temper
         ature: float) -> int:
    141 +    if not legal_moves:
    142 +        raise ValueError("no legal moves available")
    143 +    visit_array = np.asarray(visits, dtype=np.float64)
    144 +    if temperature <= 0:
    145 +        best = np.max(visit_array[legal_moves])
    146 +        best_moves = [move for move in legal_moves if visit_array[move] == best
         ]
    147 +        return int(best_moves[0])
    148 +    scaled = np.zeros_like(visit_array)
    149 +    for move in legal_moves:
    150 +        scaled[move] = visit_array[move] ** (1.0 / temperature)
    151 +    total = scaled.sum()
    152 +    if total <= 0:
    153 +        return legal_moves[0]
    154 +    probs = scaled / total
    155 +    return int(np.random.choice(np.arange(WIDTH), p=probs))
    156 +
    157 +
    158 +def visits_to_policy(visits: list[float]) -> list[float]:
    159 +    total = sum(visits)
    160 +    if total <= 0:
    161 +        return [0.0] * WIDTH
    162 +    return [float(v / total) for v in visits]

     1 +"""Policy-value network used by MCTS."""
     2 +
     3 +from __future__ import annotations
     4 +
     5 +from dataclasses import dataclass
     6 +
     7 +import torch
     8 +from torch import nn

    10 +from .constants import HEIGHT, WIDTH

    12 +
    13 +class ResidualBlock(nn.Module):
    14 +    def __init__(self, channels: int) -> None:
    15 +        super().__init__()
    16 +        self.block = nn.Sequential(
    17 +            nn.Conv2d(channels, channels, kernel_size=3, padding=1, bias=False),
    18 +            nn.BatchNorm2d(channels),
    19 +            nn.ReLU(inplace=True),
    20 +            nn.Conv2d(channels, channels, kernel_size=3, padding=1, bias=False),
    21 +            nn.BatchNorm2d(channels),
    22 +        )
    23 +        self.relu = nn.ReLU(inplace=True)
    24 +
    25 +    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    26 +        return self.relu(x + self.block(x))
    27 +
    28 +
    29 +class PolicyValueNet(nn.Module):
    30 +    def __init__(self, input_channels: int = 3, channels: int = 128, blocks: int
         = 8) -> None:
    31 +        super().__init__()
    32 +        self.stem = nn.Sequential(
    33 +            nn.Conv2d(input_channels, channels, kernel_size=3, padding=1, bias=F
        alse),
    34 +            nn.BatchNorm2d(channels),
    35 +            nn.ReLU(inplace=True),
    36 +        )
    37 +        self.backbone = nn.Sequential(*(ResidualBlock(channels) for _ in range(b
        locks)))
    38 +
    39 +        self.policy_head = nn.Sequential(
    40 +            nn.Conv2d(channels, 32, kernel_size=1, bias=False),
    41 +            nn.BatchNorm2d(32),
    42 +            nn.ReLU(inplace=True),
    43 +            nn.Flatten(),
    44 +            nn.Linear(32 * HEIGHT * WIDTH, WIDTH),
    45 +        )
    46 +        self.value_head = nn.Sequential(
    47 +            nn.Conv2d(channels, 32, kernel_size=1, bias=False),
    48 +            nn.BatchNorm2d(32),
    49 +            nn.ReLU(inplace=True),
    50 +            nn.Flatten(),
    51 +            nn.Linear(32 * HEIGHT * WIDTH, 128),
    52 +            nn.ReLU(inplace=True),
    53 +            nn.Linear(128, 1),
    54 +            nn.Tanh(),
    55 +        )
    56 +
    57 +    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
    58 +        x = self.stem(x)
    59 +        x = self.backbone(x)
    60 +        policy_logits = self.policy_head(x)
    61 +        value = self.value_head(x).squeeze(-1)
    62 +        return policy_logits, value
    63 +
    64 +
    65 +@dataclass(slots=True)
    66 +class NetConfig:
    67 +    channels: int = 128
    68 +    blocks: int = 8
    69 +
    70 +    def build(self) -> PolicyValueNet:
    71 +        return PolicyValueNet(channels=self.channels, blocks=self.blocks)

    194 -                self._table[key] = score
    203 +                self._store_bound(key, lower=score)
    204                  self._shrink_cache_if_needed()
        ⋮
    210
    202 -        self._table[key] = best
    211 +        if best <= original_alpha:
    212 +            self._store_bound(key, upper=best)
    213 +        elif best >= original_beta:
    214 +            self._store_bound(key, lower=best)
    215 +        else:
    216 +            self._table[key] = _TTEntry(best, best)
    217          self._shrink_cache_if_needed()
        ⋮
    225
    226 +    def _store_bound(self, key: tuple[int, int], lower: int | None = None, uppe
         r: int | None = None) -> None:
    227 +        entry = self._table.get(key)
    228 +        if entry is None:
    229 +            self._table[key] = _TTEntry(
    230 +                lower_bound=lower if lower is not None else -MAX_MOVES,
    231 +                upper_bound=upper if upper is not None else MAX_MOVES,
    232 +            )
    233 +            return
    234 +        if lower is not None:
    235 +            entry.lower_bound = max(entry.lower_bound, lower)
    236 +        if upper is not None:
    237 +            entry.upper_bound = min(entry.upper_bound, upper)
    238 +
    239 +
    240 +@dataclass(slots=True)
    241 +class _TTEntry:
    242 +    lower_bound: int
    243 +    upper_bound: int
    244 +

     59 +def _policy_loss(logits: torch.Tensor, target: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
     60 +    log_probs = F.log_softmax(logits, dim=-1)
     61 +    return -(target * log_probs).sum(dim=-1).mean()

     78 +def _build_loaders(dataset: GeneratedDataset, args: argparse.Namespace):
     79 +    states = torch.from_numpy(dataset.states.astype(np.float32))
     80 +    policy = torch.from_numpy(dataset.policy)
     81 +    value = torch.from_numpy(dataset.value)
     82 +    full = TensorDataset(states, policy, value)
     83 +    train_size = min(args.dataset_samples, len(full) - args.val_samples)
     84 +    val_size = min(args.val_samples, len(full) - train_size)
     85 +    if train_size <= 0 or val_size <= 0:
     86 +        raise ValueError("dataset split is empty")
     87 +    generator = torch.Generator().manual_seed(args.seed)

         enerator)
     89 +    train_loader = DataLoader(
     90 +        train_set,

     92 +        shuffle=True,
     93 +        num_workers=min(args.workers, 8),
     94 +        pin_memory=True,
     95 +        persistent_workers=args.workers > 0,

    108 +def _collect_benchmark_states(count: int, seed: int) -> list[Connect4State]:
    109 +    rng = random.Random(seed)
    110 +    states: list[Connect4State] = []
    111 +    solver = ExactSolver(cache_size=250_000)
    112 +    while len(states) < count:
    113 +        state = Connect4State()
    114 +        opening = rng.randint(4, 16)
    115 +        for _ in range(opening):
    116 +            if state.is_terminal():
    117 +                break
    118 +            scores = solver.move_scores(state)
    119 +            if not scores:
    120 +                break
    121 +            if rng.random() < 0.7:
    122 +                best = max(scores.values())
    123 +                candidates = [move for move, score in scores.items() if score =
         = best]
    124 +                move = rng.choice(candidates)
    125 +            else:
    126 +                move = rng.choice(state.legal_moves())
    127 +            state = state.play(move)
    128 +        if not state.is_terminal():
    129 +            states.append(state)
    130 +    return states

    133 +@torch.no_grad()
    134 +def _benchmark_model(
    135 +    model: PolicyValueNet,
    136 +    device: torch.device,
    137 +    states: list[Connect4State],
    138 +    sims: int,
    139 +    cache_size: int,
    140 +) -> dict[str, float]:
    141 +    solver = ExactSolver(cache_size=cache_size)
    142 +    exact_match = 0
    143 +    value_sign_match = 0
    144 +    total = 0
    145 +    for state in states:
    146 +        exact_scores = solver.move_scores(state)
    147 +        exact_best = max(exact_scores.values())
    148 +        exact_best_moves = {move for move, score in exact_scores.items() if sco
         re == exact_best}
    149 +        visits, move, _ = run_mcts(
    150 +            model,
    151 +            state,
    152 +            device=device,
    153 +            config=MCTSConfig(simulations=sims, temperature=0.0),
    154 +            add_noise=False,
    155 +        )
    156 +        if move in exact_best_moves:
    157 +            exact_match += 1
    158 +        encoded = torch.from_numpy(state.encoded()).unsqueeze(0).to(device=devi
         ce, dtype=torch.float32)
    159 +        _, value = model(encoded)
    160 +        model_sign = 0 if abs(value.item()) < 0.1 else (1 if value.item() > 0 e
         lse -1)
    161 +        exact_sign = 0 if exact_best == 0 else (1 if exact_best > 0 else -1)
    162 +        if model_sign == exact_sign:
    163 +            value_sign_match += 1
    164 +        total += 1

    222 +

         decay)
    224 +    scheduler = torch.optim.lr_scheduler.CosineAnnealingLR(optimizer, T_max=arg
         s.epochs)
    225 +    scaler = torch.amp.GradScaler(enabled=device.type == "cuda")
    226 +    log_csv = run_dir / "metrics.csv"
    227 +    log_jsonl = run_dir / "metrics.jsonl"
    228 +    best_score = -1.0
    229 +
    230 +    for epoch in range(1, args.epochs + 1):
    231 +        model.train()
    232 +        epoch_policy = 0.0
    233 +        epoch_value = 0.0
    234 +        epoch_total = 0.0
    235 +        steps = 0
    236 +
    237 +        progress = tqdm(train_loader, desc=f"epoch {epoch}/{args.epochs}", leav
         e=False)
    238 +        for states, policy_target, value_target in progress:
    239 +            states = states.to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32, non_blocking
         =True)
    240 +            policy_target = policy_target.to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32
         , non_blocking=True)
    241 +            value_target = value_target.to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32,
         non_blocking=True)
    242 +            optimizer.zero_grad(set_to_none=True)
    243 +            with torch.autocast(device_type=device.type, dtype=torch.bfloat16 i
         f device.type == "cuda" else torch.float32):
    244 +                policy_logits, value_pred = model(states)
    245 +                policy_loss = _policy_loss(policy_logits, policy_target)
    246 +                value_loss = F.mse_loss(value_pred, value_target)
    247 +                loss = policy_loss + value_loss
    248 +            scaler.scale(loss).backward()
    249 +            scaler.step(optimizer)
    250 +            scaler.update()
    251 +
    252 +            epoch_policy += float(policy_loss.item())
    253 +            epoch_value += float(value_loss.item())
    254 +            epoch_total += float(loss.item())
    255 +            steps += 1
    256 +            progress.set_postfix(loss=f"{loss.item():.4f}")
    257 +
    258 +        scheduler.step()
    259 +
    260 +        model.eval()
    261 +        val_policy = 0.0
    262 +        val_value = 0.0
    263 +        val_total = 0.0
    264 +        val_steps = 0
    265 +        exact_top1 = 0
    266 +        exact_total = 0
    267 +        with torch.no_grad():

    269 +                states = states.to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32, non_bloc
         king=True)
    270 +                policy_target = policy_target.to(device=device, dtype=torch.flo
         at32, non_blocking=True)
    271 +                value_target = value_target.to(device=device, dtype=torch.float
         32, non_blocking=True)
    272 +                policy_logits, value_pred = model(states)
    273 +                policy_loss = _policy_loss(policy_logits, policy_target)
    274 +                value_loss = F.mse_loss(value_pred, value_target)
    275 +                loss = policy_loss + value_loss
    276 +                val_policy += float(policy_loss.item())
    277 +                val_value += float(value_loss.item())
    278 +                val_total += float(loss.item())
    279 +                val_steps += 1
    280 +
    281 +                prediction = policy_logits.argmax(dim=-1)
    282 +                target = policy_target.argmax(dim=-1)
    283 +                exact_top1 += int((prediction == target).sum().item())
    284 +                exact_total += int(states.size(0))
    285 +
    286 +        benchmark = _benchmark_model(model, device, benchmark_states, args.benc
         hmark_sims, cache_size=250_000)
    287 +        metrics = {

    289 +            "train_policy_loss": epoch_policy / max(steps, 1),
    290 +            "train_value_loss": epoch_value / max(steps, 1),
    291 +            "train_loss": epoch_total / max(steps, 1),
    292 +            "val_policy_loss": val_policy / max(val_steps, 1),
    293 +            "val_value_loss": val_value / max(val_steps, 1),
    294 +            "val_loss": val_total / max(val_steps, 1),
    295 +            "val_top1": exact_top1 / max(exact_total, 1),
    296 +            "lr": optimizer.param_groups[0]["lr"],
    297 +            **benchmark,
    298 +        }
    299 +        _write_metric(log_csv, log_jsonl, metrics)
    300 +        _save_checkpoint(run_dir / "last.pt", model, optimizer, net_config, epo
         ch, metrics)
    301 +
    302 +        score = 0.7 * metrics["benchmark_best_move_acc"] + 0.3 * metrics["val_t
         op1"]
    303 +        if score > best_score:
    304 +            best_score = score
    305 +            _save_checkpoint(run_dir / "best.pt", model, optimizer, net_config,
          epoch, metrics)
    306 +
    307 +    summary = {
    308 +        "best_score": best_score,
    309 +        "run_dir": str(run_dir),
    310 +        "best_checkpoint": str(run_dir / "best.pt"),
    311 +        "play_command": f"python -m connect4_az.play --checkpoint {run_dir / 'b
         est.pt'} --human-second",
    312 +    }
    313 +    (run_dir / "summary.json").write_text(json.dumps(summary, indent=2) + "\n")
    314 +    print(json.dumps(summary, indent=2))

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• I found a more important issue than the slow test: the data generator was redundantly
  re-solving the same position for policy and value targets. I’m collapsing that into a
  single exact search per state and pushing the solved-data distribution deeper into the
  game tree, which should materially improve throughput.

  solving. I’m changing the dataset labels to use exact state values plus tactically

     30 +    while True:

     57 +def exact_tiebreak_move(state: Connect4State, solver: ExactSolver) -> int:
     58 +    scores = solver.move_scores(state)
     59 +    best = max(scores.values())
     60 +    candidates = [move for move, score in scores.items() if score == best]

         ce, dtype=torch.float32)

         lse -1)

• I’m letting the calibration run continue. At this point the only meaningful signal
  left is the first benchmarked checkpoint; anything earlier would just be more timing
  speculation.

• I’m changing the sampling strategy again, but for a clear reason: exact scores on the
  final sampled state are cheap, exact scores on every move of the rollout are not. A
  much larger exact-labeled random/non-losing dataset is a better use of the three-hour
  budget than a much smaller exact-trajectory dataset.

• Waited for background terminal · . .venv/bin/activate && python - <<'PY'
import time, torch
from connect4_az.model import PolicyValueNet
for channels, blocks in [(256,12),(320,16),(384,16)]:
    model = PolicyValueNet(channels=channels, blocks=blocks).cuda()
    x = torch.randn(256,3,6,7, device='cuda')
    opt = torch.optim.AdamW(model.parameters(), lr=1e-3)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    t0 = time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(20):
        opt.zero_grad(set_to_none=True)
        logits, value = model(x)
        loss = logits.square().mean() + value.square().mean()
        loss.backward()
        opt.step()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    dt = time.perf_counter() - t0
    print({'channels': channels, 'blocks': blocks, 'steps_per_s': round(20/dt, 2)})
PY

     1 +#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2 +set -euo pipefail

     5 +shift || true

     7 +. .venv/bin/activate
     8 +

    10 +if [[ ! -f "$CHECKPOINT" ]]; then
    11 +  CHECKPOINT="$RUN_DIR/last.pt"
    12 +fi
    13 +
    14 +if [[ ! -f "$CHECKPOINT" ]]; then
    15 +  echo "No checkpoint found in $RUN_DIR" >&2
    16 +  exit 1
    17 +fi
    18 +
    19 +have_side_flag=0
    20 +have_sims_flag=0
    21 +for arg in "$@"; do
    22 +  case "$arg" in
    23 +    --human-first|--human-second)
    24 +      have_side_flag=1
    25 +      ;;
    26 +    --sims)

    28 +      ;;
    29 +  esac

    38 +fi
    39 +

        @"

from pathlib import Path
import torch
from connect4_az.evaluate import exact_tiebreak_move
from connect4_az.game import Connect4State
from connect4_az.mcts import MCTSConfig, run_mcts
from connect4_az.play import load_checkpoint
from connect4_az.solver import ExactSolver
device = torch.device('cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu')
model, checkpoint = load_checkpoint(Path('runs/final2/last.pt'), device)
solver = ExactSolver()
for sims in (4096, 8192):
    config = MCTSConfig(simulations=sims, temperature=0.0)
    opening = Connect4State()
    _, move, _ = run_mcts(model, opening, device=device, config=config, add_noise=False)
    scores = solver.move_scores(opening)
    best = max(scores.values())
    exact_moves = sorted(move_ for move_, score in scores.items() if score == best)
    game = Connect4State()
    while not game.is_terminal():
        if game.to_play == 1:
            _, chosen, _ = run_mcts(model, game, device=device, config=config,
add_noise=False)
        else:
            chosen = exact_tiebreak_move(game, solver)
        game = game.play(chosen)
    outcome = 0 if game.winner() is None else (1 if game.winner() == 1 else -1)
    print(json.dumps({
        'checkpoint_epoch': int(checkpoint.get('epoch', 0)),
        'sims': sims,
        'opening_move': move + 1,
        'opening_move_exact': int(move in exact_moves),
        'exact_opening_moves': [m + 1 for m in exact_moves],
        'model_as_first_vs_perfect': outcome,
    }))
PY
